<div>TNN</div><div itemtype="https://schema.org/Person" itemscope="itemscope" itemprop="author"><a target="_blank" rel="author" class="auth_detail" href="/toireporter/author-Farzana-Patowari-479252641.cms">Farzana Patowari</a><meta itemprop="name" content="Farzana Patowari"></div><div data-plugin="dateformat" dateval="Updated: Aug 27, 2020, 14:41 IST">Updated: Aug 27, 2020, 14:41 IST</div><span class="clear clearfix"></span><i data-plugin="fbshare" class="as_fbicon">facebook</i><i data-plugin="twshare" class="as_twticon">twitter</i><i data-plugin="pinshare" class="as_inicon">Pintrest</i></div></div><div class="twocolum"><div class="col_box1"><div class="coverimg"><div class="coverimgIn"><img src="https://static.toiimg.com/thumb/msid-77780201,imgsize-320451,width-800,height-600,resizemode-75/77780201.jpg" data-imgid="77780201" alt="Punit J Pathak with his fiancee Nidhi" title="Punit J Pathak with his fiancee Nidhi"></div><div class="imgcaption">Punit J Pathak with his fiancee Nidhi</div></div><div class="as_article clearfix"><div class="article_content clearfix"><arttextxml><div class="section1"><div class="Normal">Choreographer and former <a class="linelink" href="https://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/topic/Khatron-Ke-Khiladi">Khatron Ke Khiladi</a> winner Punit J Pathak got engaged to his girlfriend, <a class="linelink" href="https://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/topic/Nidhi-Moony-Singh">Nidhi Moony Singh</a>, on Wednesday in an intimate ceremony in Mumbai. The couple first met on the sets of \n<i>Jhalak Dikhhla Jaa</i> but hit it off while working on \n<i>Dil Hai Hindustani</i>. Nidhi worked in the creative department of both shows. After dating for over two and a half years, Punit and Nidhi decided to get engaged. The engagement ceremony was only attended by the immediate family members.\n\n<div class="last7brdiv"></div><br>Talking about their decision to get engaged, Punit says, \xe2\x80\x9cMore than lovers, Nidhi and I are friends. We were talking about getting engaged and when we asked each other if we wanted to settle down together, we both agreed at once. The lockdown gave us a lot of time to think and we took the decision together. Our families consulted the panditji and he gave us a good date for the ceremony.\xe2\x80\x9d\n<div class="last6brdiv"></div><br>\n<div class="top2brdiv"></div><br>Punit says that all his friends were shocked because none of them knew about the ceremony. \xe2\x80\x9cPeople knew that I was dating Nidhi, but I wanted to make it official since I am fully committed to her and this relationship. I think it was the right time to do so and Nidhi agreed. It is a very big step for us and I am still digesting the fact that I am engaged. My friends have been asking about the next steps now that we are engaged,\xe2\x80\x9d laughs Punit.\n<div class="last4brdiv"></div><br>\nHe shares that wedding bells will ring soon, depending on when the current situation improves. \xe2\x80\x9cWe will decide on a wedding date soon. We want our families and friends to be a part of our big day. But it all depends on when the crisis that we are all in resolves,\xe2\x80\x9d shares Punit.\n<div class="last2brdiv"></div><br>\n<div class="last1brdiv"></div><br>\n<br>\n</div></div></arttextxml><div class="endarticlebrd clear"><span>End of the article</span></div><div class="photo_comment" id="commentmodule77779750" data-cmntstatus="true" data-cmntmsid="77779750"><div data-plugin="ascomments" class="videos_photos_md clearfix" data-msid="77779750"><h3 data-plugin="commentlabel"><i data-plugin="invokecomments" class="cmnticon photo_sprite" data-val="cmnt_block_shw">Comments <small class="cmnt_cnt_bbl">(0)</small></i></h3><div style="display:none;" class="comment_box clearfix"><div data-profile="pic" class="user_cmt_pic"><img alt="" src="https://static.toiimg.com/photo/29251859.cms?width=42&amp;height=42"></div><div class="user_cmt_box"><textarea placeholder="Add your comment here..." data-plugin="comment-textarea" class="cmt_textbox" col="50" row="4"></textarea><div class="clear"></div><input class="rate_submit_btn tvguide_submit" value="Submit" type="button"></div></div><div style="display:none;" data-plugin="obscenecmt" class="smsblock clearfix"><p>Refrain from posting comments that are obscene, defamatory or inflammatory, and do not indulge in personal attacks, name calling or inciting hatred against any community. <strong>Help us delete comments</strong> that do not follow these guidelines <strong>by marking them offensive</strong>.
